name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in October 2022
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:4.5
posted:Posted October 7, 2022
msg:The Oriental Grand hotel is part of a complex which includes 3 theme parks.  One indoor mountain park, one indoor water park, and one large outdoor theme park.  The parks were fun for our toddler.  Call in advance to see which parts of the park are open/closed for the season.  The hotel and facilities are designed for kids, so expect lots of them to be around! We stayed for 3 nights during the October Golden Week but the hotel was not overly busy, nor was the theme park.  

The breakfast was solid with mostly Chinese options but Western options as well.  We enjoyed both the breakfast and the buffet dinner.  Other food options in the area are quite limited, and the food in the parks is pretty poor.  

We were a 20-40 minute taxi ride away from other major attractions in the city, like Daxianglin and the giant buddha, as well as some of the ancient towns.

The rooms were clean and new, and we had an excellent view of the nightly fireworks show from the main theme park, even from the bathtub!  The rooms were quiet at night and the blackout curtains allowed everyone to sleep in.  The beds and pillows were very comfortable.  

Overall I would recommned this hotel to people seeking quiet and comfort during a theme-park trip.
